By Leen Randell

Updated: Feb 22, 2025

The Aspleniaceae Family

Aspleniaceae is a family of plants, commonly known as the maidenhair fern family.

It is a group of vascular plants characterized by the presence of fiddlehead fronds and sori, which are clusters of spores on the underside of the fronds. Aspleniaceae consists of approximately 130 species of ferns, many of which are native to tropical and subtropical regions around the world.

The family is often divided into two subfamilies: Asplenioidae and Cheiroglossoidae.
